<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><font face="宋体">武器提升：受到</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><font face="宋体">超合金</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><font face="宋体">Z改造的武器，该武器获得【8加骰】和【神兵】特性；并且武器伤害值提升16点，破甲值提升24点。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><font face="宋体">盔甲提升：受到</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><font face="宋体">超合金</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><font face="宋体">Z改造的盔甲，会获得【神兵】特性；并且其盔甲防御提升42点。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><font face="宋体">盾牌提升：受到</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><font face="宋体">超合金</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><font face="宋体">Z改造的盾牌，会获得【神兵】特性；并且其盾牌防御提升36点；使用该盾牌进行格挡时，免疫攻击方的加骰。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><font face="宋体">载具提升：受到</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><font face="宋体">超合金</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><font face="宋体">Z改造的载具，其装甲值提升36点；并且免疫【贯穿】和【超级贯穿】。此外，受到</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><font face="宋体">超合金</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><font face="宋体">Z改造的载具在结构值归零时只会瘫痪而不会爆炸，并且可以在瘫痪后可以按照修复规则进行维修。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; TEXT-TRANSFORM: none; COLOR: rgb(0,0,0); LETTER-SPACING: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-ansi-font-style: normal"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><!--EndFragment-->如意神珍铁<span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">改造</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">本质：魔幻本质</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font>A+4000</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">分类：材质改造</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：出自东方玄幻世界，据传由太清道德天尊亲手炼制而成的仙家奇珍，是一种可以自由变化自身体积与质量的神奇金属，通常情况下呈现出暗金色泽，即使只是一小块也有惊人的重量。当持有者握住时，表面缭绕着瑞气与霞光，挥舞时则转为煌煌大日般的闪耀金光。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">物品强化：受到如意神珍铁改造的物品，在计算其物品的硬度时，硬度增加</font>8点，同时影响该物品的结构值。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">沉重金属：使用如意神珍铁制造的物品，其重量翻倍，若原本忽略不计，则依然忽略不计。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">武器提升：武器伤害提升</font>16点，破甲提升12点，无视目标的伤害减免，获得【认主】【威猛】【魔法】【神兵】特性。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">致命一击：使用如意神珍铁制造的武器进行攻击时，若成功造成伤害，则投掷一个</font>1D10骰子，若结果为8,9,10，则本次伤害在计算目标的伤害减免等能力后，最终伤害翻倍，这是一个暴击能力。（若你拥有类似的能力，则以最终伤害为基数，分别计算）</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">无限膨胀：持有者花费一个迅捷动作，神珍铁制作的兵器将会急速膨胀，从虚无中凭空诞生出无尽质量，瞬间成长为擎天的巨大兵装，以挟山压卵之势向敌人碾去，变回来需要一个迅捷动作。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">每增加</font>1点体积，则增加10公斤，每增加6点体积，则触及增加2米。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">增强的体积是有上限的，上限为</font>X。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
